WBS Cellular Automata app generates patterns according to rules specified by the user. Sometimes very simple rules generate patterns of astonishing complexity. The patterns are generated on a two-dimensional lattice of cells. Each cell can be in one of two states: alive (on) or dead (off). A transition between the states is influenced by the cell’s neighbourhood – the eight cells surrounding the one in question.\r\n\r\nInitially, the lattice is populated randomly with alive and dead cells.
